<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вилы.html>ви́лы</a> (10026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vidla</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вилы.html>ви́лы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">víly</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вилы.html>ви́л</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>

***вильнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вильнуть.html>вильну́ть</a> (21041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вилять.html>виля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">viljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вильнуть.html>вильну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vilʹnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вилять.html>виля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wag</li>
<li>to twist, to zigzag, to make sharp turns, <i>(river)</i> to meander</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prevaricate, to be evasive</li></ol>

***вилять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вилять.html>виля́ть</a> (10982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*viljati</i>, imperfective of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*viliti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вилять.html>виля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">viljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вильнуть.html>вильну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wag</li>
<li>to twist, to zigzag, to make sharp turns, <i>(river)</i> to meander</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prevaricate, to be evasive</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подви́ливать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podvílivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***вина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина</a> (2890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vina</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">vaina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">viná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вина.html>вины́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вина.html>ви́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guilt, fault; blame</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***винегрет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́т</a> (20907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vinaigrette</i> ("a salad dressing")
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vinegrét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Vinegret.jpg/220px-Vinegret.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Vinegret.jpg/330px-Vinegret.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Vinegret.jpg/440px-Vinegret.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2640" data-file-height="2060" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́т</a></div></div></div>
<ol><li>vinaigrette, a Russian salad</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a mixture, a blending
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1967</b>,  Владимир Владимирович Набоков (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Nabokov" class="extiw" title="w:Vladimir Nabokov">Vladimir Vladimirovich Nabokov</a>),  <cite>Лолита</cite>, part 1, chapter 2 |  translation of  Vladimir Nabokov,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lolita" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lolita">Lolita</a></cite>, 1955:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отлича́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мягкость.html>мя́гкостью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдца</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:легкость.html>лёгкостью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нра́ва</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:винегрет.html>винегре́том</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ген.html>ге́нов</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:швейцарский.html>швейца́рский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданин.html>граждани́н</a>, полуфранцу́з-полуавстри́ец, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дунайский.html>дуна́йской</a> прожи́лкой.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Moj otéc otličálsja mjáxkostʹju sérdca, ljóxkostʹju nráva — i célym <b>vinegrétom</b> iz génov: byl švejcárskij graždanín, polufrancúz-poluavstríjec, s Dunájskoj prožílkoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My father was a gentle, easy-going person, a <b>salad</b> of racial genes: a Swiss citizen, of mixed French and Austrian descent, with a dash of the Danube in his veins.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>Сле́дует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговориться.html>оговори́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́л</a></span> — <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:определение.html>определе́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подходить.html>подхо́дят</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> ПВХ-содержащие <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числе́</a> — баннерная <a href = vnd.unilang:ткань.html>ткань</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:называемый.html>называ́емые</a> «фронтлит» <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> «бэклит»), самоклеящиеся <a href = vnd.unilang:пленка.html>плёнки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тка</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вино́</a> (916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vino</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīnum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wóyh₁nom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виноватый.html>винова́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vinovátyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)винова́тее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)винова́тей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guilty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:виноватый.html>винова́ты</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní <b>vinováty</b> vo vsjóm.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>are guilty</b> of everything.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">виноградъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vinogradŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calqued from Germanic (compare German <span class="Latn" lang="de">Wingert</span>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винт</a> (5367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gwint</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gewinde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vint</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винта́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>screw</li>
<li>propeller</li>
<li>vint (card game, variety of whist)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hard disk (from <i>Winchester</i>, the codename of IBM 3340 drive)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> drug addicts</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> methamphetamine</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vint</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***вира.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́ра</a> (31386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vira</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wergeld</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">víra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вира.html>ви́р</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wergeld</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́ж</a> (16448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">viráž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>виража́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>виражи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вираже́й</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bend, turn</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">viráž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́жа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вираж.html>вира́жей</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chemical solution</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***вирус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a> (8887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vírus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́руса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́русы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́русов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирусный.html>ви́русный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> virus (DNA/RNA causing disease)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> computer virus</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>With the exception of scientific or medical works, this noun is typically treated as inanimate.</li></ul>

***вирусный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вирусный.html>ви́русный</a> (15116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vírus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирусный.html>ви́русный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vírusnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> virus</li>
<li>viral</li></ol>
